	TRACEIDR = 00000026
	CONFIGR = 000000C1
		.instp0 = 0 (Trace LD & ST instructions as P0 off)
		.bb     = 0 (Branch Broadcast disabled)
		.cci    = 0 (Cycle Count instruction trace disabled)
		.cid    = 1 (Context ID trace enabled)
		.vmid   = 1 (VMID trace enabled)
		.cond   = 0 (Conditional instuction trace: disabled)
		.ts     = 0 (Global timestamp trace disabled)
		.rs     = 0 (Return Stack disabled)
		.qe     = 0 (Q element trace: disabled
		.da     = 0 (Data address trace disabled)
		.dv     = 0 (Data value trace disabled)
	STALLCTLR not implemented.
	SYNCPR = 0C
	CCCTLR = 000 (Cycle Count control)
	BBCTLR = 000 (Branch Broadcast control)
	QCTLR not implemented.

		Event0=[Single]: NEVER
		Event1=[Single]: NEVER
		Event2=[Single]: NEVER

	EVENTCTL1R = 00000000
		.insten = 0: Instr Trace event element on events - disabled
		.dataen = 0: Data trace element disabled
		.atb = 0: ATB trace trigger disabled
	TSCTLR = 00 (Event = [Single]: NEVER)

	VICTLR = 00000201 (ViewInst Event = [Single]: ALWAYS)
	.exlevel_s = 0, ELs off:[none]
	.exlevel_ns = 0, ELs off:[none]
	.ssstatus = 1 (StartStop = started)
	VIIECTLR = 00000000
	VISSCTLR = 00000000

ETMv4 dynamic configuration:

===General configuration===
	TRACEIDR = 0000002B
	CONFIGR = 000000C1
		.instp0 = 0 (Trace LD & ST instructions as P0 off)
		.bb     = 0 (Branch Broadcast disabled)
		.cci    = 0 (Cycle Count instruction trace disabled)
		.cid    = 1 (Context ID trace enabled)
		.vmid   = 1 (VMID trace enabled)
		.cond   = 0 (Conditional instuction trace: disabled)
		.ts     = 0 (Global timestamp trace disabled)
		.rs     = 0 (Return Stack disabled)
		.qe     = 0 (Q element trace: disabled
		.da     = 0 (Data address trace disabled)
		.dv     = 0 (Data value trace disabled)

	SYNCPR = 0C
	CCCTLR = 000 (Cycle Count control)
	BBCTLR = 000 (Branch Broadcast control)
	QCTLR not implemented.

	EVENTCTL1R = 00000000
		.insten = 0: Instr Trace event element on events - disabled
		.dataen = 0: Data trace element disabled
		.atb = 0: ATB trace trigger disabled
	TSCTLR = 00 (Event = [Single]: NEVER)

===General configuration===
	TRACEIDR = 0000002F
	CONFIGR = 000000C1
		.instp0 = 0 (Trace LD & ST instructions as P0 off)
		.bb     = 0 (Branch Broadcast disabled)
		.cci    = 0 (Cycle Count instruction trace disabled)
		.cid    = 1 (Context ID trace enabled)
		.vmid   = 1 (VMID trace enabled)
		.cond   = 0 (Conditional instuction trace: disabled)
		.ts     = 0 (Global timestamp trace disabled)
		.rs     = 0 (Return Stack disabled)
		.qe     = 0 (Q element trace: disabled
		.da     = 0 (Data address trace disabled)
		.dv     = 0 (Data value trace disabled)
	STALLCTLR not implemented.
	SYNCPR = 0C
	CCCTLR = 000 (Cycle Count control)
	BBCTLR = 000 (Branch Broadcast control)
	QCTLR not implemented.

		Event0=[Single]: NEVER
		Event1=[Single]: NEVER
		Event2=[Single]: NEVER
		Event3=[Single]: NEVER
	EVENTCTL1R = 00000000
